	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') != '7c5f298fb8e1b23d1005d1264938961209f6c1a9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') !== '7c5f298fb8e1b23d1005d1264938961209f6c1a9') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') !== '06e9d65ac5a8aaf898b1641755cf785d7e924b6b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') !== '7c5f298fb8e1b23d1005d1264938961209f6c1a9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '7adcdf5c4c37fcd339ea782f56d121a87aba1c3b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '7adcdf5c4c37fcd339ea782f56d121a87aba1c3b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '524f5b894f0b2bc6b353501931d2f0d2d9fa4660') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '7adcdf5c4c37fcd339ea782f56d121a87aba1c3b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
